 jin bhakton ko mantron ke uccharan yaa jaap main mushkil hoti he unke liye upasna kii sabase uttam vidhi he chalisa kaa paath
 Let's know what is the importance of Chalisa
 
 
 chalisa kaa itihaas or mahatv- saral bhashaa main kii gaiprarthana chalisakahi jaati he
 - which a devotee does to please his lord or isht
 - aamtaur par samasyaon kaa nivaaran karne ke liye chalisa kaa paath kiya jaataa he
 - It is called Chalisa because it has forty lines
 - saral bhashaa main likhi hone ke kaaran chalisa aasaani se padhi ja sakati he
 Therefore, this mode of prayer became very popular among the devotees
 - chalisa main alag-alag line kaa alag mahatv hota hai
 - Chalisa's lines are also used in special problems
 - tulsidas ji kii likhihanuman chalisasbase shaktishaalee or lokapriy maani jaati he
 Chalisa is one of the simplest methods of pleasing God
 devon ke dev hon yaa vasudev shri krishna, maa jagadamba hon yaa mahabali hanuman, sabhi devi-devataaon ko prasann karne ke liye alag chalisa rachi gai he lekin bahut kam logon ko chalisa ke paath kii uttam vidhi maaloom hoti he
 Let us know what is the best method of chalisa recitation
 
 
 - jin devi-devtaa kichalisa kaa pathakarna ho unke chitra yaa murti ke saamne baithen
 - Place a container filled with water in front of the idol
 - phir chalisa kaa paath karen, teen baar chalisa kaa paath karnaa uttam hota he
 - After the lesson, accept that water as a prasad
 - koshish karen kii chalisa paath kaa samay roj ek hi ho
 Chalisa can also be recited during travel or sleeping in special conditions
 - mantra jaap maansik ho to zyada acha he
 - But it is best to recite Chalisa by speaking or singing
 mangalvaar ko milegaa sehat kaa vardaanjyotish ke jaankaron kii maane to mahabalihanuman kii chalisaka paath sabase jaldi prabhavi hota he
 Mahabali always protects the devotee reciting Hanuman Chalisa on every Tuesday
 aaie jaanate hai mangalvaar ko kaise milegaa sehat kaa vardaan
 
 
 - Offer Tulsi Dal to Hanuman on Tuesday
 - isse aapako jivan main bharan poshan kii samasya nahin hogi
